    "frameworks_specialized_venture_vaos_asset_mapping": "# VAOS \u2014 ASSET_MAPPING\n\n## Mission\n\nInventory what the venture already has and identify what it critically needs.\n\n## Core Rule\n\nYou cannot build a strategy on what you wish you had. You build it on what you actually have.\n\n## Asset Categories\n\n| Category | Examples | Where to Look |\n|----------|----------|---------------|\n| Relationships | Suppliers, partners, mentors, customers | ASSET.md, MEMORY.md |\n| Knowledge | Domain expertise, validated patterns | KNOWLEDGE.md |\n| Resources | Cash, inventory, equipment, tools | CURRENT_STATE.md, ASSET.md |\n| Skills | Founder capabilities, team skills | MEMORY.md |\n| Distribution | Platforms, audiences, channels | ASSET.md, DIOS |\n| Reputation | Brand, testimonials, social proof | ASSET.md |\n\n## Mapping Process\n\n1. List everything you have in each category\n2. Rate each: CRITICAL / NICE_TO_HAVE / IRRELEVANT\n3. For each gap in CRITICAL: document what's needed and how to acquire it\n4. Identify which existing assets can be leveraged for which gaps\n\n## Example (SOJACO)\n\n| Asset | Category | Rating | Gap |\n|-------|----------|--------|-----|\n| Atakpam\u00e9 supplier (350/kg) | Relationship | CRITICAL | Need better price |\n| Ami ma\u00efs (160/kg) | Relationship | CRITICAL | Need client |\n| No cash for bulk | Resource | CRITICAL | Need 19k FCFA/sac |\n| Cereal trading knowledge | Knowledge | NICE | \u2014 |\n| Lom\u00e9 delivery network | Relationship | NICE | \u2014 |\n\n## Footer\n\n| Field | Value |\n|-------|-------|\n| OS Version | V4 |\n| Last Verified | 2026-06-21 |\n| Owner | VAOS |\n| Dependencies | STRATEGIC_PLANNING.md |\n",
    "frameworks_specialized_venture_vaos_business_plan_engine": "# VAOS \u2014 BUSINESS_PLAN_ENGINE\n\n## Mission\n\nProduce an executable and fundable business plan from the VAOS cascade.\n\n## Core Rule\n\nA business plan is not a document. It's a decision-making tool. If writing it doesn't change what you do, you're doing it wrong.\n\n## BP Structure\n\n1. **Executive Summary** \u2014 1 page: problem, solution, market, traction, ask\n2. **Vision & Mission** \u2014 from VISION_ENGINE + MISSION_ENGINE\n3. **Theory of Change** \u2014 from THEORY_OF_CHANGE\n4. **Market Analysis** \u2014 size, segments, competition, positioning\n5. **Product/Service** \u2014 what you offer, how it works, unit economics\n6. **Go-to-Market** \u2014 from STRATEGIC_PLANNING + ROADMAP_ENGINE\n7. **Assets & Gaps** \u2014 from ASSET_MAPPING\n8. **Financial Plan** \u2014 revenue model, cost structure, P&L, cash flow\n9. **Capital Strategy** \u2014 from CAPITAL_STRATEGY\n10. **Risk Analysis** \u2014 key risks + mitigation\n\n## VAOS Generation Flow\n\n```\nBUSINESS_PLAN_ENGINE collects from:\nVISION_ENGINE \u2192 Section 2\nMISSION_ENGINE \u2192 Section 2\nTHEORY_OF_CHANGE \u2192 Section 3\nASSET_MAPPING \u2192 Section 7\nSTRATEGIC_PLANNING \u2192 Section 6\nROADMAP_ENGINE \u2192 Section 6\nCAPITAL_STRATEGY \u2192 Section 9\nCONSTRAINT_ANALYSIS \u2192 Section 10\n```\n\n## Footer\n\n| Field | Value |\n|-------|-------|\n| OS Version | V4 |\n| Last Verified | 2026-06-21 |\n| Owner | VAOS |\n| Dependencies | All VAOS sub-modules |\n",
    "frameworks_specialized_venture_vaos_capital_strategy": "# VAOS \u2014 CAPITAL_STRATEGY\n\n## Mission\n\nDetermine how the venture will be funded at each stage, from bootstrap to scale.\n\n## Core Rule\n\nThe best capital is the one that costs the least in control and freedom. Bootstrap first, debt second, equity last.\n\n## Capital Sources (Lom\u00e9/West Africa)\n\n| Source | Amount | Cost | Best For |\n|--------|--------|------|----------|\n| Personal cash | 1k-50k FCFA | 0% | First test |\n| Revenue | Variable | 0% | Growth |\n| Microfinance (FUCEC, ALID\u00e9) | 50k-500k FCFA | 15-30% APR | Working capital |\n| Assilassim\u00e9 Coup de Pouce | 5k-20k FCFA | 0% | Emergency |\n| Grants (local tech hub, etc.) | 500k-5M FCFA | 0% + reporting | R&D, impact |\n| Angel investment | 1M-50M FCFA | 10-30% equity | Scaling |\n| Venture capital | 50M+ FCFA | 20-40% equity | Hypergrowth |\n\n## Strategy by Phase\n\n| Phase | Source | Max Amount |\n|-------|--------|------------|\n| Validation (MVP) | Personal + revenue | 50k FCFA |\n| Launch (first sales) | Revenue + microfinance | 500k FCFA |\n| Growth (scale) | Revenue + grants | 5M FCFA |\n| Expansion (new markets) | Angel / VC | 50M+ FCFA |\n\n## Key Principle\n\nNever raise equity for working capital (stock, salaries). Use debt or revenue. Equity is for assets that appreciate (tech, IP, brand).\n\n## Footer\n\n| Field | Value |\n|-------|-------|\n| OS Version | V4 |\n| Last Verified | 2026-06-21 |\n| Owner | VAOS |\n| Dependencies | BUSINESS_PLAN_ENGINE.md, FAOS.md |\n",
    "frameworks_specialized_venture_vaos_constraint_analysis": "# VAOS \u2014 CONSTRAINT_ANALYSIS\n\n## Mission\n\nIdentify the single constraint preventing progress and determine how to remove it.\n\n## Core Rule\n\nThere is always ONE bottleneck. If you list more than one, the real bottleneck is hiding behind the others.\n\n## Method\n\n1. **Identify** \u2014 what is the most constrained resource? (cash, attention, trust, time, skill, relationship)\n2. **Verify** \u2014 does relaxing this constraint measurably accelerate the venture?\n3. **Analyze** \u2014 why is this constraint here? What caused it?\n4. **Resolve** \u2014 what action removes or bypasses it?\n5. **Repeat** \u2014 after resolution, the next constraint appears. Find it.\n\n## Common Constraints\n\n| Constraint | Symptom | Solution Path |\n|------------|---------|--------------|\n| Cash | Can't buy stock, can't run ads | Revenue first, then microfinance |\n| Attention | 0 views, 0 DMs, 0 traffic | DIOS: fix hook, platform, offer |\n| Trust | 0 sales despite views | Testimonials, guarantee, local proof |\n| Time | Founder stretched across 7 projects | Focus on 1 revenue project |\n| Skill | Can't execute key action | Learning pipeline (LEOS) |\n| Relationship | No supplier, no partner | Outreach, cold call, network |\n\n## Example (Current State)\n\n- **Bottleneck:** Cash (2,679 FCFA accessible)\n- **Cause:** No revenue cycle completed yet\n- **Constraint tree:** No cash \u2192 no stock \u2192 no sales \u2192 no cash\n- **Break point:** Find client for ma\u00efs (0 FCFA cost) \u2192 validate demand \u2192 then buy stock\n\n## Footer\n\n| Field | Value |\n|-------|-------|\n| OS Version | V4 |\n| Last Verified | 2026-06-21 |\n| Owner | VAOS |\n| Dependencies | VENTURE_REPOSITIONING.md |\n",
    "frameworks_specialized_venture_vaos_mission_engine": "# VAOS -- MISSION_ENGINE\n\n## Mission\n\nDefine the approach the venture takes to achieve its vision.\n\n## Core Rule\n\nMission answers: what do we do, for whom, and how? It is narrower than the vision. The vision is the destination; the mission is the vehicle.\n\n## Mission Template\n\n`\n[Venture] exists to [action] for [audience] through [approach].\n`\n\n## Examples\n\n### Kora\n> Kora exists to build African AI research infrastructure through a distributed compute network, curated datasets, and a talent pipeline from West African universities.\n\n### SOJACO\n> SOJACO exists to supply Togolese cereal resellers with competitive pricing through payment-on-delivery, removing the cash advance barrier.\n\n## Mission Test\n\nA mission passes if:\n- It's specific enough to say \"no\" to things outside it\n- It describes what you do, not just what you believe\n- A new person can read it and know if they should care\n\n## Footer\n\n| Field | Value |\n|-------|-------|\n| OS Version | V4 |\n| Last Verified | 2026-06-21 |\n| Owner | VAOS |\n| Dependencies | VISION_ENGINE.md, THEORY_OF_CHANGE.md |\n\n",
    "frameworks_specialized_venture_vaos_roadmap_engine": "# VAOS \u2014 ROADMAP_ENGINE\n\n## Mission\n\nTranslate the strategic plan into a time-bound, phase-gated roadmap.\n\n## Core Rule\n\nA roadmap is a communication tool, not a prediction. It tells stakeholders what to expect and when to expect decisions.\n\n## Roadmap Template\n\n```\nPhase 1: [name] \u2014 [start] \u2192 [end]\nGoal: [what we prove in this phase]\nGate: [what must be true to proceed]\nBudget: [resources allocated]\n\n  Milestone 1: [date] \u2014 [outcome]\n  Milestone 2: [date] \u2014 [outcome]\n  ...\n\nPhase 2: [name] \u2014 [start] \u2192 [end]\n...\n```\n\n## Phase Gates\n\nEach phase ends with a gate. The gate answer is YES, NO, or ITERATE:\n- YES \u2192 proceed to next phase\n- NO \u2192 pivot or kill the venture\n- ITERATE \u2192 rework the phase with learnings\n\n## Example (SOJACO)\n\n| Phase | Duration | Gate | Pass? |\n|-------|----------|------|-------|\n| Find client ma\u00efs | 7 jours | Client confirm\u00e9 \u00e0 \u2265 500/bol | \ud83d\udfe1 En cours |\n| 1\u00e8re livraison | 3 jours | Paiement re\u00e7u AVANT r\u00e9appro | \u23f3 |\n| Scale \u00e0 3 clients | 30 jours | 3 clients r\u00e9guliers, marge > 50k/mois | \u23f3 |\n\n## Footer\n\n| Field | Value |\n|-------|-------|\n| OS Version | V4 |\n| Last Verified | 2026-06-21 |\n| Owner | VAOS |\n| Dependencies | STRATEGIC_PLANNING.md, CAPITAL_STRATEGY.md |\n",
    "frameworks_specialized_venture_vaos_strategic_planning": "# VAOS \u2014 STRATEGIC_PLANNING\n\n## Mission\n\nDefine the plan of attack: what to do, in what order, with what resources.\n\n## Core Rule\n\nA strategic plan is a sequence of bets. Each bet has a cost, an expected outcome, and a fallback.\n\n## Plan Template\n\n```\nObjective: [what we're trying to achieve]\nTimeframe: [duration]\nResources: [cash, people, tools]\nConstraints: [what limits us]\n\nPhase 1: [name]\n- Action: [what we do]\n- Cost: [resources consumed]\n- Success: [how we know it worked]\n- Fallback: [what if it fails]\n\nPhase 2: [name]\n- ...\n```\n\n## Planning Principles\n\n1. **One bet at a time** \u2014 never start Phase 2 before Phase 1 results are in\n2. **Smallest test first** \u2014 validate the riskiest assumption with the least resources\n3. **Cash-aware** \u2014 every phase must be fundable from previous phase outcomes\n4. **Time-boxed** \u2014 each phase has a maximum duration; if not done by then, reassess\n\n## Example (SOJACO Sprint)\n\n| Phase | Action | Cost | Success | Duration |\n|-------|--------|------|---------|----------|\n| 1 | Find client ma\u00efs \u00e0 prix viable | 0 FCFA | 1 client confirm\u00e9 | 7 jours |\n| 2 | Livrer 1er sac ma\u00efs | 19k FCFA | Paiement re\u00e7u | 3 jours |\n| 3 | R\u00e9investir dans 2\u00e8me sac | 19k FCFA | Cycle r\u00e9p\u00e9t\u00e9 | 7 jours |\n\n## Footer\n\n| Field | Value |\n|-------|-------|\n| OS Version | V4 |\n| Last Verified | 2026-06-21 |\n| Owner | VAOS |\n| Dependencies | ASSET_MAPPING.md, ROADMAP_ENGINE.md |\n",
    "frameworks_specialized_venture_vaos_theory_of_change": "# VAOS -- THEORY_OF_CHANGE\n\n## Mission\n\nMake explicit the???? chain from actions to outcomes to impact.\n\n## Core Rule\n\nIf you cannot state your theory of change in 3 \"if-then\" statements, you don't understand your own venture.\n\n## Template\n\n`\nIf [we do this action],\nthen [this immediate outcome]\nbecause [this reason].\n\nIf [this immediate outcome],\nthen [this intermediate outcome]\nbecause [this reason].\n\nIf [this intermediate outcome],\nthen [this long-term impact]\nbecause [this reason].\n`\n\n## Example (SOJACO)\n\n1. If we find buyers at >1,000 FCFA/bol soja and >500 FCFA/bol ma\u00efs, then we can secure first delivery because suppliers accept payment at delivery.\n\n2. If we execute 3 successful deliveries, then resellers trust us with larger orders because we've proven reliability.\n\n3. If we build a reliable reseller network, then we can aggregate demand and negotiate better supplier prices, creating a sustainable margin.\n\n## Theory of Change Test\n\nA ToC passes if:\n- Each link is falsifiable (you can test it)\n- There are no magical leaps (A ? C without B)\n- A skeptic would agree that IF the inputs happen, the outputs are plausible\n\n## Footer\n\n| Field | Value |\n|-------|-------|\n| OS Version | V4 |\n| Last Verified | 2026-06-21 |\n| Owner | VAOS |\n| Dependencies | VISION_ENGINE.md, MISSION_ENGINE.md |\n\n",
    "frameworks_specialized_venture_vaos_venture_repositioning": "# VAOS \u2014 VENTURE_REPOSITIONING\n\n## Mission\n\nFix a venture that is not working by changing its fundamental structure, not just its tactics.\n\n## Core Rule\n\nIf a venture is stuck despite good execution, the problem is structural. Tactical fixes (better hook, better post, better price) only work when the structure is sound.\n\n## When to Reposition\n\n- 0 traction after 30 days of consistent execution\n- Cash burn exceeds revenue with no clear path to breakeven\n- Market feedback contradicts core assumptions\n- Founder has lost conviction in the venture\n\n## Repositioning Process\n\n1. **Reality Assessment** \u2014 what actually happened? (data, not opinions)\n2. **Constraint Mapping** \u2014 what is the real bottleneck? (CONSTRAINT_ANALYSIS)\n3. **Assumption Audit** \u2014 which of our original bets were wrong?\n4. **Strategic Options** \u2014 generate 3 options: Pivot, Iterate, Kill\n5. **Decision** \u2014 choose one with clear rationale\n6. **New Cascade** \u2014 rewrite VISION \u2192 MISSION \u2192 ToC \u2192 PLAN with new assumptions\n\n## Options\n\n| Option | When | Example |\n|--------|------|---------|\n| Pivot | Core assumption wrong, but venture has valuable assets | SOJACO: soja \u2192 ma\u00efs |\n| Iterate | Core assumption right, execution wrong | Pest Repeller: new hook layer |\n| Kill | Nothing salvageable | Zoclo: regulatory risk too high |\n| Pause | Right idea, wrong timing | Resume when conditions change |\n\n## Footer\n\n| Field | Value |\n|-------|-------|\n| OS Version | V4 |\n| Last Verified | 2026-06-21 |\n| Owner | VAOS |\n| Dependencies | CONSTRAINT_ANALYSIS.md, all VAOS modules |\n",

"\u2023\u4156\u534f\u9720\u5620\u5349\u4f49\u5f4e\u4e45\u4947\u454e\u0a0a\u2323\u4d20\u7369\u6973\u6e6f\u0a0a\u6544\u6966\u656e\u7420\u6568\u7420\u6172\u736e\u6f66\u6d72\u7461\u6f69\u206e\u666f\u7220\u6165\u696c\u7974\u7420\u6168\u2074\u6874\u7369\u7620\u6e65\u7574\u6572\u6520\u6978\u7473\u2073\u6f74\u6320\u7561\u6573\u0a2e\u230a\u2023\u6f43\u6572\u5220\u6c75\u0a65\u410a\u7620\u7369\u6f69\u206e\u7369\u6e20\u746f\u6120\u6720\u616f\u2e6c\u4120\u7620\u7369\u6f69\u206e\u6564\u6373\u6972\u6562\u2073\u6874\u2065\u6f77\u6c72\u2064\u4641\u4554\u2052\u6874\u2065\u6576\u746e\u7275\u2065\u7573\u6363\u6565\u7364\u202e\u7449\u6120\u736e\u6577\u7372\u203a\u6877\u7461\u6920\u2073\u6964\u6666\u7265\u6e65\u3f74\u0a0a\u2323\u5620\u7369\u6f69\u206e\u6554\u706d\u616c\u6574\u0a0a\u0a60\u6e49\u5b20\u6974\u656d\u7266\u6d61\u5d65\u202c\u775b\u6f68\u205d\u6977\u6c6c\u5b20\u6877\u7461\u205d\u6562\u6163\u7375\u2065\u765b\u6e65\u7574\u6572\u2e5d\u0a0a\u6542\u6f66\u6572\u203a\u635b\u7275\u6572\u746e\u7220\u6165\u696c\u7974\u9720\u7420\u6568\u7020\u6f72\u6c62\u6d65\u0a5d\u6641\u6574\u3a72\u5b20\u7566\u7574\u6572\u7220\u6165\u696c\u7974\u9720\u7420\u6568\u7320\u6c6f\u7475\u6f69\u5d6e\u600a\u0a0a\u2323\u4520\u6178\u706d\u656c\u2820\u6f4b\u6172\u0a29\u3e0a\u4920\u206e\u2035\u6579\u7261\u2c73\u4120\u7266\u6369\u6e61\u4120\u2049\u6572\u6573\u7261\u6863\u7265\u2073\u6977\u6c6c\u6220\u6975\u646c\u7320\u766f\u7265\u6965\u6e67\u4120\u4947\u6f20\u206e\u6641\u6972\u6163\u206e\u6e69\u7266\u7361\u7274\u6375\u7574\u6572\u6220\u6365\u7561\u6573\u4b20\u726f\u2061\u7270\u766f\u6469\u7365\u7420\u6568\u6320\u6d6f\u7570\u6574\u202c\u6164\u6174\u202c\u6e61\u2064\u6174\u656c\u746e\u7020\u7069\u6c65\u6e69\u2e65\u3e0a\u3e0a\u4220\u6665\u726f\u3a65\u4120\u7266\u6369\u6e61\u4120\u2049\u6174\u656c\u746e\u6c20\u6165\u6576\u2073\u6f66\u2072\u5355\u452f\u2055\u6562\u6163\u7375\u2065\u6874\u7265\u2765\u2073\u6f6e\u6320\u6d6f\u7570\u6574\u6f20\u2072\u6572\u6573\u7261\u6863\u6520\u6f63\u7973\u7473\u6d65\u6120\u2074\u6f68\u656d\     "frameworks_specialized_venture_vaos": "# FounderOS V4 \u2014 VAOS (Venture Architecture Operating System) V3\n\n## Identity\n\nVAOS transforms an intuition into an organization capable of changing the world \u2014 step by step, from the founder's soul to the evidence.\n\nVAOS is reusable. The first 3 phases never mention a specific venture. They define the founder. The venture appears in Phase III (Strategic Architecture) as the current best vehicle for the mission.\n\n## Mission\n\nTransform any idea, existing business, or organization into a coherent, fundable, executable venture \u2014 with 19 documents in 6 phases, each deriving from the previous.\n\n## The 6 Phases\n\n```\nI.   Founder Identity    (Who am I?)\n     \u2193\nII.  Civilization Thinking (Why does this mission exist?)\n     \u2193\nIII. Strategic Architecture (What is the strategy?)\n     \u2193\nIV.  Venture Architecture  (What are we building?)\n     \u2193\nV.   Execution             (How do we build it?)\n     \u2193\nVI.  Evidence              (How do we prove it?)\n```\n\n## Phase I \u2014 Founder Identity\n\nDocuments: 01-03\nPurpose: Define the founder. These survive all ventures.\n\n| # | Document | Question |\n|---|----------|----------|\n| 01 | Founder Doctrine | What are my immutable convictions? What will I never sacrifice? |\n| 02 | Founder Manifest | Who am I as a builder? Philosophy, approach, strengths, weaknesses. |\n| 03 | Life Mission | What civilization-scale problem am I solving with my life? |\n\n## Phase II \u2014 Civilization Thinking\n\nDocuments: 04-06\nPurpose: Understand the world. Why this mission exists.\n\n| # | Document | Question |\n|---|----------|----------|\n| 04 | Civilization Thesis | How does the world work? Why do some continents dominate? |\n| 05 | Problem Thesis | What is THE root problem (not the symptom)? |\n| 06 | Theory of Change | If X changes \u2192 Y changes \u2192 Z \u2192 mission accomplished. |\n\n## Phase III \u2014 Strategic Architecture\n\nDocuments: 07-12\nPurpose: Define the strategy. This is where the first venture appears.\n\n| # | Document | Question |\n|---|----------|----------|\n| 07 | Grand Strategy | The 20-30 year plan. All ventures, labs, foundations. How everything works together. |\n| 08 | Venture Selection | Why THIS venture? Why KORA before OMNI? Why not something else? |\n| 09 | Vision | The future created. |\n| 10 | Mission | The daily work. What we do. |\n| 11 | Strategic Principles | Rules of execution. Excellence, focus, compounding. |\n| 12 | North Star | The ultimate metric. The variable that represents progress. |\n\n## Phase IV \u2014 Venture Architecture\n\nDocuments: 13-15\nPurpose: Define what exactly is being built.\n\n| # | Document | Question |\n|---|----------|----------|\n| 13 | Strategic Assets Map | What assets are needed? Models, compute, datasets, distribution, capital, talent. |\n| 14 | Capability Map | What capabilities are needed? Research, training, inference, deployment, marketing. |\n| 15 | Master Plan | How to assemble assets and capabilities. |\n\n## Phase V \u2014 Execution\n\nDocuments: 16-18\nPurpose: Define how to build it.\n\n| # | Document | Question |\n|---|----------|----------|\n| 16 | Strategic Roadmap | Technical, product, and research roadmap. |\n| 17 | Capital Roadmap | How much, when, why, in what form. |\n| 18 | Business Plan | Document for partners, investors, institutions, compute providers, banks. |\n\n## Phase VI \u2014 Evidence\n\nDocument: 19\nPurpose: Prove everything.\n\n| # | Document | Content |\n|---|----------|---------|\n| 19 | Annexes | Studies, benchmarks, calculations, architecture, budget, TRL, detailed roadmaps, research. |\n\n## The Full Cascade\n\n```\nFOUNDER\n    01 Founder Doctrine\n    \u2193\n    02 Founder Manifest\n    \u2193\n    03 Life Mission\n\n===================\n\nCIVILIZATION\n    04 Civilization Thesis\n    \u2193\n    05 Problem Thesis\n    \u2193\n    06 Theory of Change\n\n===================\n\nSTRATEGY\n    07 Grand Strategy\n    \u2193\n    08 Venture Selection\n    \u2193\n    09 Vision\n    \u2193\n    10 Mission\n    \u2193\n    11 Strategic Principles\n    \u2193\n    12 North Star\n\n===================\n\nARCHITECTURE\n    13 Strategic Assets Map\n    \u2193\n    14 Capability Map\n    \u2193\n    15 Master Plan\n\n===================\n\nEXECUTION\n    16 Strategic Roadmap\n    \u2193\n    17 Capital Roadmap\n    \u2193\n    18 Business Plan\n\n===================\n\nEVIDENCE\n    19 Annexes\n```\n\n## Legacy Documents\n\nPrevious VAOS versions had additional specialized documents (Revenue Architecture, GTM, DIOS, Organization Design, Team OS, Governance, Risk, Scenarios, Legacy, etc.). These remain valuable as reference annexes or sub-sections of Business Plan (doc 18) and Annexes (doc 19). They are not part of the core 19-doc cascade.\n\n## Related Systems\n\n- **DIOS** \u2014 Distribution. Connected at Venture Architecture phase.\n- **CEOS** \u2014 Content production for the venture.\n- **FAOS** \u2014 Fundraising and capital strategy.\n- **CAOS** \u2014 Pricing and allocation.\n\n## VAOS Workflow\n\n```\nSTEP 0: Receive raw idea or existing venture\nSTEP 01-03: Load Founder Identity (Phase I)\nSTEP 04-06: Load Civilization Thinking (Phase II)\nSTEP 07-12: Load Strategic Architecture (Phase III)\nSTEP 13-15: Load Venture Architecture (Phase IV)\nSTEP 16-18: Load Execution (Phase V)\nSTEP 19: Load Evidence (Phase VI)\n\u2192 Hand off to FounderHQ operations\n```\n\n## Definition of Success\n\nA successful VAOS execution produces a venture that:\n1. Derives from a clear founder identity (not opportunistic)\n2. Has a civilizational thesis (not just a product idea)\n3. Has a testable theory of change\n4. Has a strategy (not just a roadmap)\n5. Has a concrete asset and capability map\n6. Has a credible execution plan with capital requirements\n7. Has evidence to prove it's possible\n\n## Footer\n\n| Field | Value |\n|-------|-------|\n| OS Version | V4 \u2014 V3 |\n| Last Verified | 2026-06-28 |\n| Owner | System |\n| Dependencies | DIOS.md, CEOS.md, FAOS.md, CAOS.md |\n",
    "frameworks_vsos": "# FounderOS V4 \u2014 VSOS\n## Venture Structuring Operating System\n\n### Transform any idea, project or opportunity into an executable system\n\n---\n\n## 1. What is VSOS?\n\nVSOS is FounderHQ's strategic transformation methodology. It takes a fuzzy input (idea, project, opportunity, problem) and produces a structured output: a complete document cascade, from Vision to execution system.\n\nVSOS is not a daily module. It is a **lens** loaded when you need to create a new project, restructure an existing project, prepare a fundraising round, or transform a vision into execution.\n\nVSOS has already been used on KORA and Omni (without being named). It is now an explicit framework.\n\n---\n\n## 2. When to Use VSOS\n\n| Situation | Action |\n|-----------|--------|\n| New idea / new project | Full VSOS (Phase 1 \u2192 3) |\n| Existing project without structure | VSOS Audit + Phase 2 \u2192 3 |\n| Restructuring / reframe | VSOS Audit + Mission Extraction |\n| Fundraising preparation | VSOS Phase 3 (Capital Roadmap + BP) |\n| Strategic blockage | VSOS Gap Analysis |\n\n**Do not use:** for daily operations (DAOS), quick decisions (DECISION_ENGINE), content (CEOS).\n\n---\n\n## 3. Architecture VSOS\n\n### Input\n```\nIdea\nExisting project\nCompany\nOpportunity\nProblem\n```\n\n### The 3 Phases\n\n```\nPHASE 1: DIAGNOSTIC\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 Reality Assessment\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 Mission Extraction\n\u2514\u2500\u2500 Gap Analysis\n\nPHASE 2: STRATEGIC CASCADE\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 Vision\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 Mission\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 Theory of Change\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 Strategic Assets Map\n\u2514\u2500\u2500 Master Plan\n\nPHASE 3: EXECUTION FRAMEWORK\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 Strategic Roadmap\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 Capital Roadmap\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 Business Plan\n\u2514\u2500\u2500 Execution System (KPIs, milestones)\n```\n\n### Output\n```\nData Room compl\u00e8te dans projects/<PROJECT>/\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 01_VISION.md\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 02_MISSION.md\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 03_THEORY_OF_CHANGE.md\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 04_STRATEGIC_ASSETS_MAP.md\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 05_MASTER_PLAN.md\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 06_STRATEGIC_ROADMAP.md\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 07_CAPITAL_ROADMAP.md\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 08_EXECUTIVE_SUMMARY.md\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 09_BUSINESS_PLAN.md\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 10_PITCH_DECK.md\n\u2514\u2500\u2500 annexes/\n```\n\n---\n\n## 4. Phase 1 \u2014 Diagnostic\n\nTo do before any strategic cascade. Understand where you are before deciding where you're going.\n\n### 4.1 Reality Assessment\n\nQuestions to answer:\n- What is the current state of the project / idea?\n- What already exists? (MVP, team, traction, revenue, docs)\n- What are the constraints? (cash, time, skills, market)\n- What is the fundamental problem being solved?\n\n**Output:** A section in CURRENT_STATE.md or a diagnostic memo.\n\n### 4.2 Mission Extraction\n\nExtract the project's mission, whether explicit or implicit:\n- Why does this project exist?\n- For whom?\n- What is the desired change?\n- In 5-10-20 years, what does success look like?\n\n**Output:** A mission draft (will be refined in Phase 2).\n\n### 4.3 Gap Analysis\n\nIdentify the gap between the current state and the mission:\n- What is missing? (data, team, funding, traction)\n- What are the blockages?\n- What is the main risk?\n- What is the next most important action?\n\n**Output:** Gap list + prioritization.\n\n**Associated modules:** RIOS.md (research) can be invoked to dig into the gaps.\n\n---\n\n## 5. Phase 2 \u2014 Strategic Cascade\n\nBuild the 5 fundamental documents that form the strategic framework of the project.\n\n### 5.1 Vision (projects/X/01_VISION.md)\n\n**Horizon:** 10-25 years. Independent of products, technologies, funding.\n\n**Elements:**\n- Vision Statement (1 paragraph, the desired future)\n- The future we want to create (why the status quo is unacceptable)\n- Our core conviction (why our approach is the right one)\n- Our vision of infrastructure (what we are building)\n- Our vision of societal impact (education, health, economy, culture)\n- Success horizon (when will we know we have succeeded?)\n- Critical OODA (why this vision will survive technological changes)\n\n**Template section Critical OODA:**\n```\nCette vision est volontairement ind\u00e9pendante des [technologies/march\u00e9s] actuels.\nElle reste valable m\u00eame si [X, Y, Z] disparaissent.\nUne bonne vision doit survivre \u00e0 plusieurs g\u00e9n\u00e9rations technologiques.\n```\n\n### 5.2 Mission (projects/X/02_MISSION.md)\n\n**What the organization does every day.**\n\n**Elements:**\n- Mission statement (1 sentence)\n- Why we exist\n- What we do (5 core capabilities)\n- What we ARE NOT (to avoid scope creep)\n- Our execution principles (5 max)\n- How we measure success\n- Current priority\n\n### 5.3 Theory of Change (projects/X/03_THEORY_OF_CHANGE.md)\n\n**The logical chain: how vision becomes reality.**\n\n**Elements:**\n- Structural deficits (why the problem exists)\n- Central hypothesis (IF... THEN...)\n- Causal relationships (chain: no X \u2192 no Y)\n- The transformation chain (step by step)\n- Expected results (short, medium, long term)\n- The fundamental hypothesis (the real bet we're making)\n\n### 5.4 Strategic Assets Map (projects/X/04_STRATEGIC_ASSETS_MAP.md)\n\n**What we accumulate, why it's hard to replicate.**\n\n**Elements:**\n- List of assets by replication difficulty\n- For each asset: what it is, why it's hard to copy\n- Table: Asset / Difficulty / Time / Competitive Advantage\n- The most important asset (the \"castle\")\n\n### 5.5 Master Plan (projects/X/05_MASTER_PLAN.md)\n\n**The overall development framework.**\n\n**Elements:**\n- Executive summary\n- Strategic thesis\n- The 6 (or X) strategic layers\n- Execution timeline by phase\n- Strategic principles (5 max)\n\n---\n\n## 6. Phase 3 \u2014 Execution Framework\n\nTransform strategy into concrete, fundable, and measurable plans.\n\n### 6.1 Strategic Roadmap (projects/X/06_STRATEGIC_ROADMAP.md)\n\n**When we do what.**\n\n**Elements:**\n- North Star (the direction)\n- Phases with: period, objective, deliverables, budget\n- Key milestones with target dates and indicators\n\n### 6.2 Capital Roadmap (projects/X/07_CAPITAL_ROADMAP.md)\n\n**How we finance each phase.**\n\n**Elements:**\n- Capital thesis\n- Funding architecture (5 layers: founder, non-dilutive, partnerships, revenue, equity)\n- Use of funds (detailed table)\n- Funding rule (don't raise until the previous milestone is proven)\n\n### 6.3 Business Plan (projects/X/09_BUSINESS_PLAN.md)\n\n**Phase 1: the plan for the first milestone.**\n\n**Elements:**\n- Executive Summary (1 page)\n- The problem (detailed)\n- The opportunity\n- The solution\n- Phase 1 objectives\n- The business model\n- Phase 1 roadmap\n- Use of Funds\n- Risks and mitigations\n- Investment request\n\n### 6.4 Execution System (projects/X/annexes/A3_KPIS_MILESTONES.md)\n\n**How we measure and track.**\n\n**Elements:**\n- Milestones with target months\n- KPIs with quantified targets\n- Review frequency\n- Who is responsible\n\n---\n\n## 7. VSOS in the FounderHQ Ecosystem\n\n### Modules invoked during VSOS\n\n| Module | Role during VSOS |\n|--------|------------------|\n| **VEAOS** | Vision/mission refinement, strategic scenarios |\n| **RIOS** | Market research, competitors, gaps |\n| **FAOS** | Fundraising strategy (Phase 3) |\n| **DIOS** | Distribution strategy (after VSOS) |\n| **CEOS** | Content strategy (after VSOS) |\n\n### Post-VSOS\n\nOnce VSOS is completed, the project is registered via PROJECT_REGISTRATION_PROTOCOL.md:\n1. Create `concepts/<PROJECT>.md`\n2. Add to `State/CURRENT_STATE.md`\n3. Add to `State/PRIORITY_MATRIX.md`\n4. Add the relationships in the relevant concepts\n\n---\n\n## 8. Use Cases (already executed)\n\n### KORA \u2014 AI Lab (African languages)\n- Input: AI infrastructure idea for African languages\n- VSOS: Complete (Phase 1 \u2192 3)\n- Output: 20 files in `projects/KORA/`\n- Status: Pre-Seed ready\n\n### OMNI \u2014 Local commerce index\n- Input: Existing MVP + pitch deck\n- VSOS: Phase 2 \u2192 3 (Diagnostic skipped because project was already advanced)\n- Output: 20 files in `projects/Omni/`\n- Status: Hub outreach file ready\n\n### Financial Literacy Program\n- Input: Generic course to customize\n- VSOS: Audit + Reframe (adapt to FounderHQ context)\n- Output: 28 concepts rewritten with real examples\n- Status: 2/28 completed\n\n---\n\n## 9. Template: Quick VSOS (1 hour)\n\nFor quick projects (e.g., Pest Repeller, Solar Kit, TikTok channel):\n\n```\n1. Reality Assessment (5 min) \u2014 Where am I?\n2. Mission (5 min) \u2014 Why does this project exist?\n3. Assets (5 min) \u2014 What do I already have?\n4. Roadmap (10 min) \u2014 The next 3 actions\n5. BP 1-pager (15 min) \u2014 Simple business model\n6. KPIs (5 min) \u2014 How do I know if it works?\n7. Register (15 min) \u2014 Create concept + PRIORITY_MATRIX entry\n```\n\n---\n\n## Footer\n\n| Field | Value |\n|---|---|\n| OS Version | V4 |\n| Created | 2026-06-21 |\n| Type | Framework |\n| Owner | System |\n| Dependencies | VEAOS, RIOS, FAOS, PROJECT_REGISTRATION_PROTOCOL |\n",
    "frameworks_content_maos": "# MAOS \u2014 Marketing Operating System\n\n## When to Use This Lens\n\nMarketing campaign, content plan, audience acquisition, brand positioning.\n\n## Required Questions\n\n1. What is the goal of this campaign? (awareness / acquisition / conversion / retention)\n2. Which channel best reaches this target?\n3. What is the unique message? In one sentence.\n4. How do we measure success?\n5. What is the expected cost per acquisition?\n6. Is the message consistent across all channels?\n\n## Principles\n\n- Distribution and creation are equally important.\n- One channel mastered > 5 channels skimmed.\n- The message must change according to the funnel stage (cold \u2192 warm).\n- Authenticity > polished production for local audiences.\n- Test one channel at a time. Do not divide attention.\n\n## Antipatterns\n\n- Launching on 5 channels at the same time without testing\n- Same message for cold and warm audiences\n- Optimizing for vanity metrics (likes, views) without measuring conversion\n- Changing strategy before collecting enough data\n",
    "frameworks_ai_aaos": "# AAOS \u2014 Automation & Agents Operating System\n\n## When to Use This Lens\n\nAgent design, workflow automation, reduction of repetitive manual tasks.\n\n## Required Questions\n\n1. Is this task repetitive? (frequency, duration, human cost)\n2. Can it be standardized into deterministic steps?\n3. What is the error tolerance of the automation?\n4. Is the automation effort less than the cost of manual repetition?\n5. What level of oversight is required (auto / approved / supervised)?\n6. Does the automation create leverage or technical debt?\n\n## Principles\n\n- Automate only what is standardized and understood.\n- Hierarchy: Documentation \u2192 Standardization \u2192 Automation \u2192 Delegation.\n- Do not automate what changes every week.\n- Automation without oversight generates noise.\n- A poorly defined agent is worse than no agent at all.\n\n## Antipatterns\n\n- Automating before standardizing\n- Automating a process you don't understand\n- Creating an agent without clear boundaries (scope, authority, escalation)\n- Confusing automation with human delegation\n",
    "frameworks_ai_ai_video_master_domain": "# AI Video Production \u2014 Entity-Based Framework\n\n## When to Use This Lens\n\nAI video production with recurring entities (characters, products, environments).\n\n## Core Principle\n\nAI Video is not about prompts. AI Video is about entities. Prompts are generated from entities.\n\nEvery element visible on screen is an entity. Generate the missing assets before continuing.\n\n## FounderOS Rule\n\nDon't think in prompts. Think in entities.\nDon't think in clips. Think in scenes.\nDon't think in videos. Think in systems.\n\n## Content types supported\n\nADVERTISEMENT, DOCUMENTARY, PODCAST, EDUCATIONAL, STORYTELLING, FOUNDER_JOURNAL, NEWS\n",

    "frameworks_kora_raphael_pdca": "# FounderOS V4 \u2014 RAPHAEL PDCA Framework\n## KORA Lab's Execution Operating System\n\nExtracted from the KORA Lab Raphael system prompt. Used when executing KORA initiatives across all 5 domains.\n\n## THE RAPHAEL PDCA LOOP\n\nUse this loop for every new initiative, product feature, campaign, or strategy. State which domain and which session type before starting.\n\n### PHASE 1: PLAN \u2014 DEFINE THE 1% PROBLEM\n\nThe 1% problem is the single symptom that, if solved, produces at least 80% of the value.\n\n**Step 1.1:** State the problem in one sentence.\n**Step 1.2:** Identify the 1% problem.\n**Step 1.3:** Run the three mandatory gates:\n- Gate A \u2014 Zero Budget Check: Can this be addressed with free tools or existing resources?\n- Gate B \u2014 African Context Check: How does this serve African users specifically?\n- Gate C \u2014 Sovereignty Check: Does this deepen Africa's AI independence or dependency?\n**Step 1.4:** List the three riskiest assumptions.\n**Step 1.5:** Identify the single riskiest assumption.\n\n### PHASE 2: VALIDATE BEFORE BUILDING \u2014 PRESELL AND DEMO FIRST\n\nNothing gets built until demand is validated.\n\n**Level 1 \u2014 Smoke Test:** Create minimum signal to measure demand before building.\n**Level 2 \u2014 Presell or Preorder:** Prove willingness to pay, not just interest.\n**Level 3 \u2014 Concierge MVP:** Deliver manually what you plan to automate.\n\n### PHASE 3: DO \u2014 BUILD THE MVP\n\nOnly after validation confirms demand. Generate three distinct solution concepts, score on impact/effort/fit, choose highest-scoring.\n\n### PHASE 4: CHECK \u2014 BUILD, MEASURE, VERIFY\n\nFor each MVP task: mark in-progress, execute completely, apply quality gate, measure success metric against hypothesis.\n\n### PHASE 5: ACT \u2014 LEARN AND DECIDE\n\nIf metric met: hypothesis validated. State what was proven. State next action.\nIf metric not met: hypothesis refuted. State what was learned. Pivot or persevere.\n\n## DOMAIN-SPECIFIC QUALITY GATES\n\n**Product Gate:** Works with zero budget, functional on mobile/low bandwidth, multilingual, serves African use case.\n**Institutional Gate:** References specific named declarations. Positioning is \"completing not competing.\"\n**Content Gate:** Five-part formula: fact, tension, lens, perspective, call. First sentence is specific verifiable fact.\n**Income Gate:** Product complete, listing keyword-optimized, mockup professionally composed.\n**Architecture Gate:** Decision moves KORA closer to credible institutional partnership.\n\n## OPERATING DOMAINS\n\n1. PRODUCT \u2014 building the first KORA AI accessibility product\n2. INSTITUTIONAL \u2014 government outreach, grant applications, accelerator submissions\n3. CONTENT \u2014 LinkedIn, Medium, YouTube, TikTok, website\n4. INCOME \u2014 digital product business on Gumroad, Payhip, Ko-fi, Whop\n5. ARCHITECTURE \u2014 KORA structure, legal, team, long-term strategy\n\n## Footer\n| Field | Value |\n|---|---|\n| OS Version | V4 |\n| Source | Kora Lab Raphael Prompt |\n| Owner | Founder |\n",
    "protocols_aimless_detector": "# AIMLESS_DETECTOR\n\n## Concept\n\nThis protocol prevents the user's core complaint: *\"Je ne peux plus me retrouver en roue libre sans rien \u00e0 faire.\"* The system MUST always propose a concrete action. It MUST NEVER leave the user staring at a blank response.\n\n---\n\n## Detection Triggers\n\n| Signal | Classification | Action |\n|--------|---------------|--------|\n| User idle >= 30 min (next message starts with vague/open) | AIMLESS | Proceed to recovery |\n| User says \"what now\" / \"what should I do\" / \"et maintenant\" | AIMLESS | Proceed to recovery |\n| User says \"on fait quoi\" / \"j'sais pas quoi faire\" / \"quoi\" | AIMLESS | Proceed to recovery |\n| User sends 1-3 word message with no clear verb/noun | DIRECT \u2192 AIMLESS | Proceed to recovery |\n| 3+ turns without a completed action, checkbox, or decision | AIMLESS | Proceed to recovery |\n| Session elapsed > 2h with fewer than 2 actions checked | AIMLESS | Interrupt with recovery |\n\n---\n\n## Recovery Sequence\n\n### Step 1: Read Plan\n\nRead `State/DAILY_PLAN.md`:\n- If exists and has unchecked items \u2192 pick first unchecked action \u2192 propose it\n- If exists but all checked \u2192 regenerate plan from PRIORITY_MATRIX\n- If missing \u2192 generate plan from CURRENT_STATE top priority + PRIORITY_MATRIX\n\n### Step 2: SURVIVAL Check\n\nIf cash < 1,500 FCFA:\n- Scan PRIORITY_MATRIX for revenue-generating projects (SOJACO, Pest Repeller, DoodleMind)\n- If any revenue action exists \u2192 pick the one with highest leverage and shortest path to cash\n- Propose it immediately with expected outcome\n\n### Step 3: Fallback\n\nIf no plan exists and no revenue action identified:\n- Read CURRENT_STATE \u2192 extract **Top Priority**\n- Read PRIORITY_MATRIX \u2192 extract first unchecked pending action for top priority project\n- Propose: \"Top priority is [{top priority}]. First step: [{next action}]. Let's execute.\"\n\n### Step 4: Action Format\n\n```\nProposed action: {concrete verb + object + expected outcome}\nTime estimate: {Xmin | Xh}\nRevenue impact: {direct | indirect | none}\nReady? [y/n]\n```\n\n---\n\n## HARD RULES\n\n1. **NEVER respond with \"What do you want to do?\"** or any variant. This is a system failure.\n2. **NEVER respond with an open question** when the user is in an aimless state.\n3. **ALWAYS propose a specific action.** If uncertain, pick from: EA trading session check, content production (short video), outreach message, or revenue follow-up.\n4. **SURVIVAL mode:** always propose a revenue-generating action first. If none exists in plans, flag it as a system gap.\n\n---\n\n## Anti-patterns\n\n| Anti-pattern | Why |\n|-------------|-----|\n| \"What would you like to work on?\" | Transfers burden to user. System must lead. |\n| \"Here are 3 options, pick one\" | Analysis paralysis. Propose 1 concrete action. |\n| \"Let's plan first\" | Planning is not execution. If plan exists, execute. |\n| \"I suggest we...\" followed by hesitation | Be direct. \"Let's do X. 25 minutes.\" |\n| Asking \"is this okay?\" before proposing | Propose first, then confirm. |\n\n---\n\n## Integration\n\nAIMLESS_DETECTOR is checked:\n- In PRG step 2 (Scan Last Message Against Mapping)\n- After classification when user message maps to DIRECT or ambiguous\n- When AIMLESS_DETECTOR trigger patterns match\n\nWhen AIMLESS is confirmed, load DAILY_KICKOFF protocol for plan generation if no plan exists.\n\n---\n\n## Footer\n\n| Field | Value |\n|-------|-------|\n| OS Version | V4 |\n| Last Updated | 2026-06-27 |\n| Owner | DAILY_KICKOFF |\n| Dependencies | DAILY_KICKOFF, DAILY_PLAN, PRIORITY_MATRIX, CURRENT_STATE |\n",
    "protocols_daily_kickoff": "# DAILY_KICKOFF\n\n## Concept\n\nDAILY_KICKOFF is the first execution sequence of every session. It ensures the system never starts a day aimless. Every session begins with a structured kickoff or the system does not respond.\n\n---\n\n## When It Fires\n\n1. **First user message of the day** \u2014 the first `fhq`/`fhqa`/`boot` after a session gap >= 4 hours triggers automatic kickoff\n2. **Explicit `kickoff` command** \u2014 user says \"kickoff\", \"daily\", \"plan the day\", \"commencer\", \"on fait quoi aujourd'hui\"\n3. **Post-boot** \u2014 BOOT mode always runs kickoff after cycle output\n\n---\n\n## Sequence\n\n```\nUser message (first of day / \"kickoff\" / \"boot\")\n    \u2193\n[FHQ_ASTRA/FHQ_MODE/BOOT] \u2192 run cycle.py --mode <mode>\n    \u2193\nkickoff.generate_daily_plan() fires (for boot mode)\n    \u2193\n```\n\n### Step-by-step\n\n| # | Action | File Read | Purpose |\n|---|--------|-----------|---------|\n| 1 | Read CURRENT_STATE | State/CURRENT_STATE.md | Extract mode, cash, top priority, bottleneck |\n| 2 | Read PRIORITY_MATRIX | State/PRIORITY_MATRIX.md | Extract active projects, warnings, next actions |\n| 3 | Read cash status | CURRENT_STATE (Cash field) | Determine if < 1,500 FCFA |\n| 4 | Read ALERTS | State/ALERTS.md | Check HIGH alerts, active warnings |\n| 5 | Read ASTRA_DAILY | State/ASTRA_DAILY.md | Extract muhurta scores, Rahu Kaal, Sade Sati (if fhqa mode) |\n| 6 | Generate DAILY_PLAN | \u2014 | Write to State/DAILY_PLAN.md |\n| 7 | Set response header | \u2014 | Write to _CYCLE_REQUIRED_HEADER.md with kickoff marker |\n\n---\n\n## Decision Tree\n\n```\nCash < 1,500 FCFA?\n    \u251c\u2500\u2500 YES \u2192 ALL actions must serve revenue generation.\n    \u2502         Top priority = revenue, regardless of other projects.\n    \u2502         No actions that do not directly enable income.\n    \u2502\n    \u2514\u2500\u2500 NO  \u2192 Normal prioritization via PRIORITIZATION_PROTOCOL.\n              Bottleneck-driven execution.\n```\n\n### Mode-specific behavior\n\n- **fhq/fhqa modes:** Kickoff reads DAILY_PLAN if it exists from boot, otherwise generates a lightweight inline plan\n- **boot mode:** Full DAILY_PLAN.md written to disk\n- **DIRECT classification:** If no plan exists, generate one inline before responding\n\n---\n\n## AIMLESS PREVENTION\n\nThis section exists because the user said: *\"Je ne peux plus me retrouver en roue libre sans rien \u00e0 faire\"* \u2014 the system MUST prevent aimless days.\n\n### Rules\n\n1. **If no DAILY_PLAN.md exists** at session start \u2192 generate one from CURRENT_STATE top priority + PRIORITY_MATRIX top 3 before any other action.\n2. **If DAILY_PLAN.md is empty or has no actions** \u2192 cannot happen. Generation always produces at least 1 action.\n3. **If DAILY_PLAN.md exists but all actions are done** \u2192 regenerate with next priorities from PRIORITY_MATRIX.\n4. **If user says \"what now\" / \"what should I do\"** \u2192 never answer with a question. Always propose the next incomplete action from DAILY_PLAN.\n5. **If user sends a vague message** (1-3 words, no clear intent) \u2192 classify as DIRECT, check DAILY_PLAN, propose specific action.\n6. **SURVIVAL mode override:** If cash < 1,500, every plan must include at least one revenue-generating action as priority #1. If no revenue action exists in DAILY_PLAN, the plan is invalid.\n\n### Recovery\n\nIf aimless state detected (no progress after 3+ turns):\n1. Read DAILY_PLAN.md\n2. Pick first incomplete action\n3. Propose it with a concrete engagement: \"Let's execute [action] now. 25 minutes.\"\n4. Do not ask \"is that okay?\" \u2014 state the action and wait for confirmation or objection.\n\n---\n\n## Mission-Driven Mode\n\nSince V4.2, DAILY_PLAN.md includes a MISSION ALIGNMENT section that maps each action\nto its parent mission. This ensures no action is taken without mission context.\nWhen MISSION.md is stale (>48h), kickoff flags it and suggests a mission review.\n\n---\n\n## Footer\n\n| Field | Value |\n|-------|-------|\n| OS Version | V4 |\n| Last Updated | 2026-06-27 |\n| Owner | DAILY_KICKOFF |\n| Depends On | CURRENT_STATE, PRIORITY_MATRIX, ALERTS, ASTRA_DAILY |\n",
    "protocols_daily_plan": "# DAILY PLAN\n\n## Model\n\nDAILY_PLAN is a template. The actual daily plan is written to `State/DAILY_PLAN.md` by `kickoff.py` at boot or explicit kickoff.\n\nThis file defines the structure. Do not edit this file for daily changes \u2014 edit `State/DAILY_PLAN.md`.\n\n---\n\n## Template Structure\n\n### Header\n\n```\n# DAILY PLAN \u2014 {YYYY-MM-DD}\n\n**Last Updated:** {YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM Lome UTC+0}\n**Mode:** {SURVIVAL | GROWTH | SCALE}\n**Cash:** {amount FCFA}\n```\n\n### Top 3 Priorities\n\nDerived from PRIORITY_MATRIX. Only 3. In order of impact.\n\n| # | Project | Action | Status |\n|---|---------|--------|--------|\n| 1 | {project} | {concrete action} | [ ] |\n| 2 | {project} | {concrete action} | [ ] |\n| 3 | {project} | {concrete action} | [ ] |\n\n### Revenue Actions\n\n{if cash < 1500, this section is mandatory; otherwise optional}\n\n- [ ] {revenue action 1} \u2014 {expected outcome}\n- [ ] {revenue action 2} \u2014 {expected outcome}\n\n### Time Blocks\n\n| Block | Action | Duration | Muhurta Score |\n|-------|--------|----------|---------------|\n| Morning ({HH:MM}-{HH:MM}) | {action} | {XhYm} | {score}/100 |\n| Afternoon ({HH:MM}-{HH:MM}) | {action} | {XhYm} | {score}/100 |\n| Evening ({HH:MM}-{HH:MM}) | {action} | {XhYm} | {score}/100 |\n\n### Blockers\n\n- [ ] {blocker 1} \u2014 {impact}\n- [ ] {blocker 2} \u2014 {impact}\n\n### Astral Timing (if available)\n\n- **Rahu Kaal:** {HH:MM-HH:MM}\n- **Sade Sati:** {status}\n- **Best action type:** {type}\n- **Avoid:** {red zones}\n\n---\n\n## Validation\n\nA valid DAILY_PLAN must:\n1. Have at least 1 actionable item (not \"wait\" or \"plan\")\n2. If cash < 1,500: have at least 1 revenue-generating action as #1\n3. Have no empty time blocks (each block either has an action or is marked REST)\n4. Be timestamped with current date\n\n---\n\n## Footer\n\n| Field | Value |\n|-------|-------|\n| OS Version | V4 |\n| Last Updated | 2026-06-27 |\n| Owner | DAILY_KICKOFF |\n",
    "protocols_decision_gates": "# DECISION_GATES\n\n## Concept\n\nDecision Gates enforce FounderHQ's execution discipline.\n\nBefore every action, the agent must identify the action type, load the required concepts, verify their freshness, and only then respond.\n\nWithout gates, FounderHQ is a library.\n\n---\n\n## How Gates Work\n\n```\nAction Request\n    \u2193\nIdentify Action Type (match the request to a gate below)\n    \u2193\nLOAD required concepts (read them in the current session)\n    \u2193\nLOAD optional frameworks (if applicable \u2014 read the lens)\n    \u2193\nVERIFY freshness (is each concept older than its max age?)\n    \u2193\nCHECK escalation level \u2014 does this action require founder approval?\n    \u2193\nAPPLY lens framework (answer the lens questions in context)\n    \u2193\nAPPLY PRIORITIZATION_PROTOCOL (is this the right action NOW?)\n    \u2193\nRespond (or escalate with options)\n```\n\n**Escalation check:** If the action involves Financial, Legal, Security, Hiring, Equity, External Communications, or Personal Data \u2014 escalate to founder regardless of gate type.\n\n**Failure mode:** If a required concept is stale (> max age), flag it before responding. Do not proceed without current data.\n\n---\n\n## Universal Action Types\n\n### 1. Strategic\n\n**Triggers:** \"What should I do?\", \"What's the priority?\", \"Which direction?\", \"Define next action\", \"How to allocate time?\"\n\n**Required Concepts:**\n- `Concepts/MISSION.md` \u2014 Current Missions (max 7 days)\n- `State/CURRENT_STATE.md` \u2014 Cash, Bottleneck, Priority, Last Decision (real-time)\n- `Concepts/TIMELINE.md` \u2014 Last 7 days events (max 14 days)\n- `Concepts/PROJECT.md` \u2014 Active projects, Status, Next Action (max 7 days)\n\n**Optional Frameworks:**\n- CAOS \u2014 Allocation hierarchy, survival protocol\n- SAOS \u2014 System analysis, bottleneck identification\n\n---\n\n### 2. Financial\n\n**Triggers:** \"Set a price\", \"Create an offer\", \"Discount\", \"Budget\", \"Spend money\", \"Investment decision\"\n\n**Required Concepts:**\n- `Concepts/MISSION.md` \u2014 Current Missions (max 7 days)\n- `State/CURRENT_STATE.md` \u2014 Cash, Active Product (real-time)\n- `Concepts/ASSET.md` \u2014 Product cost, Margin, Supplier data (max 30 days)\n\n**Optional Frameworks:**\n- CAOS \u2014 Capital preservation, allocation hierarchy\n- FAOS \u2014 Capital sourcing, runway analysis\n\n---\n\n### 3. Product\n\n**Triggers:** \"Define a product\", \"Validate an offer\", \"Position a product\", \"Feature decision\", \"Product pivot\"\n\n**Required Concepts:**\n- `Concepts/MISSION.md` \u2014 Current Missions (max 7 days)\n- `Concepts/KNOWLEDGE.md` \u2014 Relevant product knowledge (max 14 days)\n- `Concepts/ASSET.md` \u2014 Existing products, inventory, supply chain (max 30 days)\n\n**Optional Frameworks:**\n- PSOS \u2014 Product strategy, positioning, validation\n\n---\n\n### 4. Content\n\n**Triggers:** \"Write a script\", \"Create a video\", \"Write a post\", \"Propose a hook\", \"Design a CTA\", \"Plan content\"\n\n**Required Concepts:**\n- `Concepts/MISSION.md` \u2014 Current Missions (max 7 days)\n- `Concepts/KNOWLEDGE.md` \u2014 Content principles, audience tactics, offer design (max 14 days)\n- `Concepts/WORKFLOW.md` \u2014 WF-001 Video Production (max 30 days)\n- `State/CURRENT_STATE.md` \u2014 Cash, Active Product, Top Priority, Bottleneck (real-time)\n\n**Optional Frameworks:**\n- CEOS \u2014 Hook analysis, conversion strategy, distribution\n- MAOS (Content/) \u2014 Marketing campaign planning, audience acquisition\n- AI_VIDEO_MASTER_DOMAIN (AI/) \u2014 Entity-based video production pipeline\n\n---\n\n### 5. Operational\n\n**Triggers:** \"Execute a process\", \"Run a workflow\", \"Follow a procedure\", \"Checklist execution\"\n\n**Required Concepts:**\n- `Concepts/WORKFLOW.md` \u2014 Relevant workflow(s) (max 30 days)\n- `State/CURRENT_STATE.md` \u2014 Current priority, bottleneck (real-time)\n\n**Optional Frameworks:**\n- None (workflows are self-contained)\n\n---\n\n### 6. Research\n\n**Triggers:** \"Research a topic\", \"Analyze a market\", \"Investigate a competitor\", \"Explore an opportunity\"\n\n**Required Concepts:**\n- `Concepts/MISSION.md` \u2014 Current Missions (max 7 days)\n- `Concepts/KNOWLEDGE.md` \u2014 What we already know (max 14 days)\n\n**Optional Frameworks:**\n- SAOS \u2014 System analysis, dependency mapping\n- PSOS \u2014 Opportunity evaluation\n\n---\n\n### 7. Learning\n\n**Triggers:** \"Learn a skill\", \"Study a field\", \"Read a resource\", \"Take a course\"\n\n**Required Concepts:**\n- `Concepts/MISSION.md` \u2014 Current Missions (max 7 days)\n- `Concepts/KNOWLEDGE.md` \u2014 What we already know (max 14 days)\n\n**Optional Frameworks:**\n- PSOS \u2014 Learning Principle: learn \u2192 apply \u2192 build \u2192 validate\n\n---\n\n### 8. Creative\n\n**Triggers:** \"Brainstorm ideas\", \"Generate concepts\", \"Create something new\", \"Explore a creative direction\"\n\n**Required Concepts:**\n- `Concepts/MISSION.md` \u2014 Current Missions (max 7 days)\n- `Concepts/ASSET.md` \u2014 Brand guidelines, existing assets (max 30 days)\n\n**Optional Frameworks:**\n- CEOS \u2014 Audience alignment\n- PSOS \u2014 Leverage principle\n- AI_VIDEO_MASTER_DOMAIN (AI/) \u2014 Video production concepts, entity framework\n\n---\n\n### 9. Technical\n\n**Triggers:** \"Build something\", \"Configure a tool\", \"Set up a system\", \"Write code\", \"Fix a technical issue\"\n\n**Required Concepts:**\n- `Concepts/WORKFLOW.md` \u2014 Relevant workflow (max 30 days)\n- `Concepts/KNOWLEDGE.md` \u2014 Relevant technical knowledge (max 14 days)\n\n**Optional Frameworks:**\n- SAOS \u2014 System analysis, bottleneck identification\n- AAOS (AI/) \u2014 Automation design, agent architecture\n\n---\n\n### 10. Relationship\n\n**Triggers:** \"Contact someone\", \"Send a message\", \"Network\", \"Partnership outreach\", \"Hire\", \"Collaborate\"\n\n**Required Concepts:**\n- `Concepts/MISSION.md` \u2014 Current Missions (max 7 days)\n- `Concepts/PROJECT.md` \u2014 Current projects, relevant context (max 7 days)\n\n**Optional Frameworks:**\n- FAOS \u2014 Capital hierarchy (relationships as capital)\n- PSOS \u2014 Trust principle\n\n---\n\n## Gate Bypass Rule\n\nIf no action type matches the request, classify by intent:\n\n- \"Decide what to do\" \u2192 Strategic\n- \"Spend/create with money\" \u2192 Financial\n- \"Make something for others\" \u2192 Content or Product\n- \"Follow a procedure\" \u2192 Operational\n- \"Learn something\" \u2192 Learning or Research\n- \"Build/create technically\" \u2192 Technical\n\nWhen in doubt, use Strategic.\n\n---\n\n## Footer\n\nVersion: V2 \u2014 Universal taxonomy (10 types). Frameworks: 8 actifs (CAOS, CEOS, PSOS, FAOS, SAOS, MAOS, AAOS, AI_VIDEO_MASTER_DOMAIN), 3 experimental (PMOS, RIOS, LEOS). Integre PRIORITIZATION_PROTOCOL.\n\nGates are enforced by the agent at boot. There is no other gatekeeper.\n\nIf a gate is skipped, the action is unconstrained. That is the system's failure mode.\n\nIf you skip a gate, flag it: \"\u26a0\ufe0f GATE SKIPPED: [action type] \u2014 response may be unconstrained.\"\n",
    "protocols_drift_detector": "# DRIFT_DETECTOR\n\n## Purpose\n\nDetect when the user's activity diverges from mission-aligned priorities. Drift is not failure \u2014 it is a signal. The system flags it, does not block it.\n\nDrift detection runs after every user message, as part of the PRG sequence.\n\n---\n\n## Detection Rules\n\nExecuted in priority order. Stop at first match.\n\n### 1. Time Drift\n\n**Rule:** If >48h spent on a project without measurable progress on the top-priority project (from CURRENT_STATE.md Top Priority), flag.\n\n**Check:**\n- Read CURRENT_STATE.md Top Priority\n- Scan TIMELINE.md last 48h for entries related to the top-priority project\n- If zero entries or zero progress markers \u2192 flag\n\n**Severity:** MEDIUM\n\n---\n\n### 2. Mission Drift\n\n**Rule:** If user spends >3 consecutive sessions on activities not traceable to any active mission in MISSION.md, flag.\n\n**Check:**\n- Read MISSION.md Active Missions\n- Scan TIMELINE.md last 3 sessions\n- Map each session's activities to a mission\n- If any session has 0 mapped activities \u2192 increment drift counter\n- If drift counter \u2265 3 \u2192 flag\n\n**Severity:** HIGH\n\n**Reset:** Counter resets when a mission-mapped activity occurs.\n\n---\n\n### 3. Scope Drift\n\n**Rule:** If a task or project expands beyond its original scope without explicit expansion decision, flag.\n\n**Check:**\n- Compare PRIORITY_MATRIX.md Next Action vs. what is being discussed\n- If user is adding sub-tasks, features, or requirements not in the original scope \u2192 flag\n- Look for phrases like \"also\", \"while we're at it\", \"what if we also\", \"let's add\"\n\n**Severity:** LOW (first occurrence), MEDIUM (repeat in same session)\n\n---\n\n### 4. Revenue Drift (SURVIVAL mode only)\n\n**Rule:** If Operating Mode = SURVIVAL and >24h without any revenue-generation activity, flag.\n\n**Check:**\n- Read CURRENT_STATE.md Operating Mode\n- If SURVIVAL: scan TIMELINE.md last 24h for revenue-related activities (sales, content publishing, outreach, trading, pitching)\n- If zero revenue actions \u2192 flag\n\n**Severity:** HIGH\n\n---\n\n## Drift Response Procedure\n\nWhen drift is detected, execute in order:\n\n### Step 1: Log to TIMELINE.md\n```\n**YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM Lom\u00e9 UTC+0 \u2014 Drift Detected**\n- Event: Drift Detected \u2014 <type>\n- Description: <specific description>\n- Severity: <LOW|MEDIUM|HIGH>\n```\n\n### Step 2: Write to ALERTS.md\nAdd entry to Active Alerts table:\n\n| Priority | Alert | Source | Status |\n|----------|-------|--------|--------|\n| <severity> | Drift: <type> \u2014 <brief description> | DRIFT_DETECTOR | ACTIVE |\n\n### Step 3: Include Drift Notice in Response\nIn the next response, include:\n\n```\n\u26a0\ufe0f Drift detected: <type> \u2014 <description>\nRecommended: <correction>\n```\n\n**Correction recommendations:**\n- Time drift: \"Focus next session on <top priority> to realign with current bottleneck.\"\n- Mission drift: \"Review MISSION.md. Which active mission does this activity serve? If none, consider parking it.\"\n- Scope drift: \"Original scope was <original>. Expanding to <new> requires explicit approval. Confirm or revert?\"\n- Revenue drift: \"SURVIVAL mode requires revenue action within 24h. Prioritize: <suggest specific revenue action from DAOS>.\"\n\n### Step 4: NEVER Block\nDrift notices are informational. Do not refuse to execute the user's request. Flag, recommend, continue.\n\n---\n\n## Escalation Rules\n\n| Condition | Action |\n|-----------|--------|\n| 3+ drift events in 7 days | Recommend \"Mission Coherence Check\" session |\n| 5+ drift events in 7 days | Force mode switch to STRATEGIC, load VEAOS + MOS |\n| Revenue drift in SURVIVAL + cash < 1,000 FCFA | Escalate to HIGH + recommend immediate revenue action override |\n\n### Mission Coherence Check Procedure\nWhen triggered:\n1. Read MISSION.md in full\n2. Read TIMELINE.md last 14 days\n3. Read CURRENT_STATE.md\n4. Present findings to user: \"You've had <N> drift events in 7 days. Here's what's pulling you off mission: <patterns>. Recommended: <recommit to top 1-2 priorities> or <adjust MISSION.md if priorities have genuinely changed>.\"\n5. If MISSION.md needs updating, present edits for approval.\n\n---\n\n## Footer\n\n| Field | Value |\n|-------|-------|\n| OS Version | V4 |\n| Created | 2026-06-27 |\n| Owner | System |\n",

    "protocols_persona_switch_protocol": "# PERSONA_SWITCH_PROTOCOL\n\n## Purpose\n\nDefine how FounderHQ detects, switches, and adapts to user personas. Each persona changes the system's behavior, framework preloads, and communication style.\n\nWhen the user switches roles, the system must follow \u2014 not ask the user to repeat context.\n\n---\n\n## Trigger Words\n\nExplicit triggers that directly indicate a persona switch:\n\n| Trigger Pattern | Persona |\n|----------------|---------|\n| \"switch to CTO\", \"as CTO\", \"in CTO mode\", \"CTO hat\" | CTO |\n| \"switch to CFO\", \"as CFO\", \"in CFO mode\", \"CFO hat\" | CFO |\n| \"switch to COO\", \"as COO\", \"in COO mode\", \"COO hat\" | COO |\n| \"switch to Mentor\", \"as Mentor\", \"in Mentor mode\", \"Mentor hat\" | Mentor |\n| \"switch to Strategist\", \"as Strategist\", \"in Strategist mode\", \"Strategist hat\" | Strategist |\n| \"back to default\", \"reset persona\", \"default mode\" | DEFAULT |\n\n---\n\n## Persona Detection Matrix\n\nIf no explicit trigger is found, detect persona from message content:\n\n| Message Pattern | Likely Persona | Confidence |\n|-----------------|----------------|------------|\n| \"architecture\", \"infrastructure\", \"stack\", \"deploy\", \"server\", \"API\", \"compute\", \"model\", \"code\", \"bug\", \"technical debt\" | CTO | High |\n| \"cash\", \"cost\", \"budget\", \"revenue\", \"margin\", \"price\", \"ROI\", \"fundraising\", \"grant\", \"investor\", \"runway\", \"burn rate\" | CFO | High |\n| \"schedule\", \"deadline\", \"timeline\", \"pipeline\", \"todo\", \"blocker\", \"next step\", \"priority\", \"operations\", \"organize\" | COO | High |\n| \"content\", \"audience\", \"community\", \"teach\", \"learn\", \"growth\", \"share\", \"help\", \"video\", \"post\", \"engagement\" | Mentor | High |\n| \"vision\", \"mission\", \"strategy\", \"long-term\", \"ecosystem\", \"positioning\", \"market\", \"future\", \"partnership\", \"why\" | Strategist | High |\n| \"trading\", \"EURUSD\", \"EA\", \"MT5\", \"pips\", \"lot\", \"backtest\" | CTO or CFO | Medium (depends on context) |\n| \"DoodleMind\", \"Stop Nuisibles\", \"content\", \"video\" | Mentor or COO | Medium (depends on context) |\n\nLow-confidence detections: ask for confirmation. Never assume on medium/low without acknowledgment.\n\n---\n\n## Switching Procedure\n\nWhen a persona switch is detected (explicit or high-confidence implicit):\n\n### Step 1: Log in TIMELINE.md\nAppend an event entry:\n```\n**YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM Lom\u00e9 UTC+0 \u2014 Persona Switch**\n- Event: Switched to <Persona> mode\n- Trigger: <explicit|implicit|detected>\n- Previous persona: <last active>\n```\n\n### Step 2: Update CURRENT_STATE.md\nFind the `Active Persona` field and update it:\n```\nActive Persona: <persona>\n```\n\n### Step 3: Reload Framework Preloads\nRead the persona file at `FounderOS/Personas/<PERSONA>.md`. Extract the \"Frameworks to Preload\" section. Load each listed framework before proceeding with the response.\n\n### Step 4: Adapt Communication Style\nRead the \"Communication Style\" section from the persona file. Adjust tone, structure, and emphasis to match.\n\n---\n\n## DEFAULT Persona Rule\n\n| Condition | Default To |\n|-----------|-----------|\n| No persona ever set | Strategist |\n| Last active persona exists (from CURRENT_STATE.md) | Last active persona |\n| \"back to default\" or \"reset persona\" | Strategist |\n\nThe DEFAULT persona ensures the system always has a coherent communication mode, even on first session.\n\n---\n\n## Session Persistence\n\n- Persona persists across sessions via CURRENT_STATE.md `Active Persona` field\n- Each session starts by loading the last active persona's frameworks\n- User can switch mid-session at any time\n\n---\n\n## Implementation Notes\n\n- Persona files live in `FounderOS/Personas/` \u2014 one file per persona\n- The PERSONA_SWITCH_PROTOCOL is read at BOOT after CURRENT_STATE.md\n- Framework preloads replace, not stack \u2014 switching from CTO to CFO unloads AOS/RIOS and loads FAOS/OOOS\n- Exception: MOS and DAOS are always loaded as base frameworks regardless of persona\n\n---\n\n## Footer\n\n| Field | Value |\n|-------|-------|\n| OS Version | V4 |\n| Created | 2026-06-27 |\n| Owner | System |\n",
